  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f4228ec7-25dd-4c13-bc95-29cf85b58382'
      });
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer15145305439254073019">When it comes to children's books, it's hard to beat the bestselling team of author Laura Numeroff and illustrator Felicia Bond for creative and captivating tales that are both fun and educational. They continue the tradition that began with such whimsical titles as <i>If You Give a Mouse a Cookie</i> and <i>If You Give a Moose a Muffin</i> with yet another tale of actions and consequen</span>
  <span id="freeText15145305439254073019" style="display:none">When it comes to children's books, it's hard to beat the bestselling team of author Laura Numeroff and illustrator Felicia Bond for creative and captivating tales that are both fun and educational. They continue the tradition that began with such whimsical titles as <i>If You Give a Mouse a Cookie</i> and <i>If You Give a Moose a Muffin</i> with yet another tale of actions and consequences: <i>If You Give a Pig a Pancake.</i> Once again, Numeroff follows the potential effects of one creature's chaotic demands, creating a tale filled with beguiling characters, delightful anticipation, and a fun sense of adventure. <br /><p><br />In addition to being humorous and entertaining, <i>If You Give a Pig a Pancake</i> allows children to see how their own constant demands might frazzle their parents. Kids should also enjoy studying the subtleties in Bond's colorful illustrations, such as the facial expressions of the book's adorable protagonist or the details found in a mountain of bubbles and the contents of a closet. Easy to understand, stimulating to both mind and eye, and irresistibly amusing, this is one book children will likely want to read over and over again. <br /></p><p>
  <br />
  <i>--Beth Amos</i>
</p></span>

<div id="review_1629293506" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1629293506" />
    <a title="Josh Caporale" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5687551-josh-caporale"><img alt="Josh Caporale" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431172307p2/5687551.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1629293506?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Josh Caporale" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Josh Caporale" href="/user/show/5687551-josh-caporale">Josh Caporale</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1629293506" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7818659623144045445">THESE are the kinds of children's books I enjoy and feel that children should be reading or having read to them! This is a modern classic that is placed in the series of books that includes "If You Give a Mouse a Cookie" and "If You Give a Moose a Muffin." The pig is quite adorable, while also being quite f</span>
  <span id="freeText7818659623144045445" style="display:none">THESE are the kinds of children's books I enjoy and feel that children should be reading or having read to them! <div id="review_1530375881" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1530375881" />
    <a title="Becca Wilson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/43279345-becca-wilson"><img alt="Becca Wilson" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1530375881?book_show_action=true">Jan 29, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Becca Wilson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Becca Wilson" href="/user/show/43279345-becca-wilson">Becca Wilson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1530375881" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3056821326390110767">If You Give a Pig a Pancake is a thrilling story about what would happen if you were to give a pig a pancake, and although it seems harmless, this story proves that you would be in for quite the day. The pig would probably want syrup, then a bath, new clothes, to tap dance, wear a costume, send a letter, take a picture, and eventually want a pancake all over again! The main theme of this story is that sometimes when you have lots of demands for someone, it can get crazy and that person gets tire</span>
  <span id="freeText3056821326390110767" style="display:none">If You Give a Pig a Pancake is a thrilling story about what would happen if you were to give a pig a pancake, and although it seems harmless, this story proves that you would be in for quite the day. The pig would probably want syrup, then a bath, new clothes, to tap dance, wear a costume, send a letter, take a picture, and eventually want a pancake all over again! The main theme of this story is that sometimes when you have lots of demands for someone, it can get crazy and that person gets tired.<br /><br />I love this story because I personally love pigs, and I think the little illustrations are absolutely hilarious. The pig's facial expressions are so cute, and the illustrations make the story seem that much crazier. I love it when picture books have funny illustrations and I found myself laughing out loud several times while reading this because of the pig's crazy antics.<br /><br />I would recommend this book to young children, because the story will captivate them and keep them focused, since you are constantly anxious about what happens next. I think this story can also teach young children that their actions affect other people, and can lead to a discussion about using manners and asking for favors instead of demanding them.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3056821326390110767" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer14666959624130863963">Good grief, after my nephew shoved this book in my face the fourth time I gave it a whirl. I'm glad I did. The combination of detail in the art and the sweat surrealism in the story made me turn the pages not to convince my nephew, but because I wanted to see where it was going(embarrassing considering it's a children's book!). My nephew enjoyed it and so did I and that's why I recommend you get a copy and find out just what happens If You Give a Pig a Pancake.</span>

    <a title="Paige Scott" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/58892814-paige-scott"><img alt="Paige Scott" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1740457916?book_show_action=true">Aug 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Paige Scott" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Paige Scott" href="/user/show/58892814-paige-scott">Paige Scott</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/58892814-paige-scott?shelf=book-summaries">book-summaries</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1740457916" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12969678187766296822">1)	This kid-friendly fiction book sends the child’s imagination soaring with the detailed pictures and creative storyline of the girl eating pancakes with a pig. This story goes from the girl and the pig eating pancakes to the pig wanting to take a bath and the series of events continues until in the end the pig wants some more pancakes and the girl is so tired because of the day that they have had. <br/>2)	Ages 0-5, Kindergarten<br/>3)	This book could be used as a first time reader for children with easy</span>
  <span id="freeText12969678187766296822" style="display:none">1)	This kid-friendly fiction book sends the child’s imagination soaring with the detailed pictures and creative storyline of the girl eating pancakes with a pig. This story goes from the girl and the pig eating pancakes to the pig wanting to take a bath and the series of events continues until in the end the pig wants some more pancakes and the girl is so tired because of the day that they have had. <br />2)	Ages 0-5, Kindergarten<br />3)	This book could be used as a first time reader for children with easy words to pronounce, and not many words on each page to intimidate them. <br />4)	Students that are just learning to read might benefit from reading this book <br />5)	This book could be used in small group as a use of learning how to read as previously stated, and children could help each other sound out the words, and work together to read the book. Then at the end of the small groups, everyone could share in front of the class how their literature circle learned to read it as a team.<br />6)	This book could be used in whole class use and read aloud to the class to introduce cause and effect, with the pages always leaving you hanging on what the pig and the girl are about to do and you could have students guess before you turn the page. For example, the pig gets sticky and the girl says then she will want to take a bath, so letting your students guess before gets their minds thinking creatively about what could happen next to the pig. <br />7)	Genre: Fiction, and related books are If You Give A Mouse A Cookie, If You Give A Moose A Muffin, etc. There is a whole series that could be used with literature circles, and each group read one of the books out of the series.<br />8)	There is a audio CD on Amazon with the whole series of books on it which may be beneficial for a classroom.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12969678187766296822" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer9917240816161301220">1) Book summary, in your own words (3 pts)<br/>-If You Give a Pig a Pancake is a story about what happens when, like like the title suggests, give a pig a pancake. This little pig gets a pancake, but that's not enough she wants some maple syrup to go with it. However, the syrup made the pig sticky so now he needs a bath.. with bubbles, but the bubbles make him want a toy, so the little girl has to go find a rubber toy for the pig, which happens to be a little duck.   <span id="freeText9917240816161301220" style="display:none">1) Book summary, in your own words (3 pts)<br />-If You Give a Pig a Pancake is a story about what happens when, like like the title suggests, give a pig a pancake. This little pig gets a pancake, but that's not enough she wants some maple syrup to go with it. However, the syrup made the pig sticky so now he needs a bath.. with bubbles, but the bubbles make him want a toy, so the little girl has to go find a rubber toy for the pig, which happens to be a little duck. The toy duck makes the pig homesick and then she feels the need for even more things. Needless to say, if you give a pig a pancake, your house will be a mess and you will lose half of your stuff. <br />2) Grade level, interest level, lexile (1 pt)<br />-Kindergarten-2nd grade.<br />3) Appropriate classroom use (subject area) (1 pt)<br />-Fun entertainment. <br />4) Individual students who might benefit from reading (1 pt)<br />-Students who love animals<br />-Students who enjoy comedies<br />5) Small group use (literaturecircles) (1 pt)<br />-Students can read through book together (or look through pictures depending on age and reading level) and talk about their favorite part, determine parts of the plot, etc.<br />6) Whole class use (read aloud) (1 pt)<br />-Carpet read aloud.<br />-Would be cool to read before a class field trip to a farm.<br />7) Related books in genre/subject or content area (1 pt)<br />-If You Give a Mouse a Cookie by Laura Numeroff<br />-If You Give a Dog a Donut by Laura Numeroff<br />8) Multimedia connections (audio book, movie) available (1 pt)<br />-Youtube Video (audio book)<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VtKx7vTQwpM">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VtKx7...</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1228950252" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17502080753563834100"> I really enjoyed reading this book "If You Give a Pig a Pancake" to my cousin, who loves reading and listening to books. We owned this book. When I was a kid I enjoyed it very much. I still think it is a great book. All children would love to read.<br/><br/> This story is about a pig who wants some pancakes, then some syrup, and the pig would keep asking for more things throughout the book. At the end of the book the pig ends up wanting more pancakes. This makes the reader wonder what the pig might want </span>
  <span id="freeText17502080753563834100" style="display:none"> I really enjoyed reading this book "If You Give a Pig a Pancake" to my cousin, who loves reading and listening to books. We owned this book. When I was a kid I enjoyed it very much. I still think it is a great book. All children would love to read.<br /><br /> This story is about a pig who wants some pancakes, then some syrup, and the pig would keep asking for more things throughout the book. At the end of the book the pig ends up wanting more pancakes. This makes the reader wonder what the pig might want next. This makes it feel like a never ending book. It shows a lot of excitement in the book. <br /><br /> The main character of this book was the pig. The pig was used throughout the whole book. There was also the little girl that would try to keep up to the pig.<br /><br /> This book took place during the summer or fall months. The book showed pictures inside of the book that are acquainted with summer and fall. And it took place at the little girl’s home.<br /><br /> I believe this book would be good for younger children. I would read it when I was little. My younger cousins also loved the book. I think it would be a great book to read to any child. This book could be a good bonding time if you read it to your child.<br /></span>

<div id="review_539582514" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/539582514" />
    <a title="Katie Paciga" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4904537-katie-paciga"><img alt="Katie Paciga" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1328506392p2/4904537.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/539582514?book_show_action=true">Feb 18, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie Paciga" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie Paciga" href="/user/show/4904537-katie-paciga">Katie Paciga</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4904537-katie-paciga?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4904537-katie-paciga?shelf=prek-2">prek-2</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer539582514" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2752360388762660839">This is a story about a little girl who tries to satisfy the desires of a pig. The story begins when the little girl gives the pig a pancake and snowballs from there. Next, the pig wants syrup and then she gets sticky so she'll need a bath. The story goes on and on and eventually ends up where she [the pig] wants more pancakes, which leaves the reader feeling like it's a never-ending story. The illustrations by Felicia Bond present the little pig's actions fairly well, but the layout can be conf</span>
  <span id="freeText2752360388762660839" style="display:none">This is a story about a little girl who tries to satisfy the desires of a pig. The story begins when the little girl gives the pig a pancake and snowballs from there. Next, the pig wants syrup and then she gets sticky so she'll need a bath. The story goes on and on and eventually ends up where she [the pig] wants more pancakes, which leaves the reader feeling like it's a never-ending story. The illustrations by Felicia Bond present the little pig's actions fairly well, but the layout can be confusing for children because multiple scenes are presented on each two-page spread (hence only 3 stars).<br /><br />I can't help but thing of "The Song that Never Ends" from Lamb Chop's Play Along (a television program for young children (here's a youtube video of the song from the program <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VZNaecq_rpU">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=VZNaec...</a> - good luck getting that one out of your head!). All of Numeroff's If You Give...series have similiar circular plot structures. This one is my favorite of the series with If You Give a Moose a Muffin coming in a close second place.<br /><br />I found this lesson idea on TeachingBooks.net. It suggests using the book as a foundation for an economics lesson (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.kidseconposters.com/literature-connection/economic-wants/if-you-give-a-pig-a-pancake/?back=literature">http://www.kidseconposters.com/litera...</a>). I'd expand on some of the conversation starters and actually have 2-3rd graders do a research project in which they determine how much money the girl would need to fulfill the wants of the pig.<br /><br />The published lexile for this title is 570 and the guided reading level is G, indicating that a child in grades 2-3 should be able to read it independently. "If You Give A Pig A Pancake" would be appropriate for a read aloud PreK-2.</span>
  <a data-text-id="2752360388762660839" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3285975026" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3285975026" />
    <a title="Samantha Ocampo" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/83328713-samantha-ocampo"><img alt="Samantha Ocampo" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3285975026?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Samantha Ocampo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Samantha Ocampo" href="/user/show/83328713-samantha-ocampo">Samantha Ocampo</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/83328713-samantha-ocampo?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/83328713-samantha-ocampo?shelf=animals">animals</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/83328713-samantha-ocampo?shelf=picture-books">picture-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3285975026" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14187055110122909647">A very amusing read for young readers, because of how much the pig is running around all over her house and through the yards. I love all of these “If you give a…” books because you can see how much one thing relates to another and is reminding the animal of something else. This can even help young readers with comparing different items together and how things are like one another as well. The illustrations are also very fun to look at because they use the white paper as the background of the de</span>
  <span id="freeText14187055110122909647" style="display:none">A very amusing read for young readers, because of how much the pig is running around all over her house and through the yards. I love all of these “If you give a…” books because you can see how much one thing relates to another and is reminding the animal of something else. This can even help young readers with comparing different items together and how things are like one another as well. The illustrations are also very fun to look at because they use the white paper as the background of the depictions. This allows the scenes to take over the entire page so the readers can see everything that the pig and girl are doing together. I also really like the style of the writing throughout the book because of how the author repeats the whole ‘if you do this, then this will happen’. It seems like an exciting little rhythm to following along through the book. I would recommend this book to young readers who want an exciting adventure.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14187055110122909647" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1883191018" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10063716748300212700">This was a cute picture book. I loved the fact that when the pig got one thing it led to a whole bunch of different things. I don't really have much to say about it except that the artwork was beautiful and now I'm interested in checking out her other stories. </span>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WQeRhG+r2EXxn6GUxTYQy5AX7SS/hNoMva55fOiTgqK1Y3gBe5WQxgfR9/l9pPaUfrncy5Utb+iWKqURcqdrng==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('UFbY54k8ngeCAJYpFJKAz3aSWGfmINWCcgfspEQZGky8MjFinQLWhHROwESsAGaQmDxpiMyJYGZZgzDJ3i3zcA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

Laura grew up as the youngest of three girls, surrounded by art, music, and books. An avid animal lover, Laura has always wanted to write a book about service dogs. She now lives in Los Angel</span>
  <span id="freeText5495490737035922419" style="display:none">Laura Joffe Numeroff is the <i>NYT</i> best-selling author of <i><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/767680.If_You_Give_a_Mouse_a_Cookie" rel="nofollow noopener">If You Give a Mouse a Cookie</a>, </i><i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/776391.What_Mommies_Do_Best_What_Daddies_Do_Best" rel="nofollow noopener">What Mommies/Daddies Do Best</a>

Laura grew up as the youngest of three girls, surrounded by art, music, and books. An avid animal lover, Laura has always wanted to write a book about service dogs. She now lives in Los Angeles, California.</span>
